  return coroutine.resume( func, ... )

   _ttbCollectGlobals = false;

   _ttbCollectGlobals = true;

function ttFixupLua50Script( t )                                           
    t = string.gsub(t, "%f[%w]for ([ %w,_]+) in +([%w_.]+) +do%f[%W]", "for %1 in pairs( %2 ) do");
    return t;                                                              
end

 : COLOR;

silhouetteSize; 
 float4x4
WorldXf;
   // obj->world
 float4x4  ViewProjX;
   // obj->clip
 float4x4
modelViewXf;   // obj->view
 float4x4
ViewWorldXf;   // obj->viewWorld
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT VS_main( float4 inPos: POSITION0, float3 inNormal: NORMAL0,float2 inTexCoord : TEXCOORD0, float3 inNomral2 : NORMAL1 ) 
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT Out;
float4 inPosScale
= ( 1.0f - silhouetteSize );
float4 worldPos
= mul( inPos,  WorldXf  );
   float4 mapper
= {0.5f , 0.5f , 0.0f , 0.0f  };
   float4 mapperA
= {1.0f , 1.0f , 0.0f , 0.0f  };
   // transform normal
float4 worldViewNormal
= mul( inNormal,  modelViewXf  );
float4 scaledNormal
= -worldViewNormal * inPosScale;
float4 worldNormalOffset
= mul( scaledNormal,  ViewWorldXf  );
float4 finalWorldPos
= worldPos    + worldNormalOffset;
Out.Pos
= mul( finalWorldPos,  ViewProjX  );
float4 normEnv  = mul( inNomral2,  modelViewXf  );
    
float4 normEnvN = normalize(normEnv);
normEnvN = normEnvN + mapperA;
    
normEnvN = normEnvN * mapper;
Out.TexCoord.x  = normEnvN.x;
Out.TexCoord.y  = (mapperA.x - normEnvN.y);
Out.vDiffuse
= materialColor;
Out.TexCoord1
= inTexCoord;
return Out;

outlineOffset
struct VS_OUTPUT_QUANT
float4 Pos           : POSITION0;
float4 vDiffuse
 : COLOR;
float2 TexCoord      : TEXCOORD0;
float2 TexCoord1     : TEXCOORD1;
 float4x4  ViewProjX;
   // obj->clip
 float4    light0Pos;
    
 float4    light1Pos;
    
 float4    lightDir;
    
 float4    materialColor;
 float     light0Intensity;
 float     light1Intensity;
 float     ambientLightIntensity;
 float
lightDirIntensity;
// bone palette
 float4x4  bonesPalette[18];
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT VS_main( float4 inPos: POSITION0, float3 inNormal: NORMAL0,float2 inTexCoord : TEXCOORD0, 
  float3 blendWeight: BLENDWEIGHT0, float4 blendIndices : COLOR)
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT Out;
float4 scaler
= {64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f };
float4 scaledIndices
blendIndices * scaler;
float4 skinPos 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
float4 skinPos1 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
float4 skinPos2 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalPos = skinPos + skinPos1 + skinPos2;
Out.Pos       =  mul( skinFinalPos,  ViewProjX  );
float3 lightVector0 = (light0Pos - inPos);
float3 lightVectorN0 = normalize(lightVector0);
float3 lightVector1 = (light1Pos - inPos);
float3 lightVectorN1 = normalize(lightVector1);
// compute lighting
float  diffuse
= (max(0,dot(inNormal,lightVectorN0)) * light0Intensity);
float  diffuse1
= (max(0,dot(inNormal,lightVectorN1)) * light1Intensity);
float  directional
= (max(0,dot(inNormal,lightDir.xyz))  * lightDirIntensity);
Out.TexCoord.x
= min(1.0f, (diffuse + diffuse1 + directional + ambientLightIntensity));
Out.TexCoord.y
= 0.0f;
Out.vDiffuse
= materialColor;
Out.TexCoord1
= inTexCoord;
return Out;

= silhouetteColor;
   // done here
return Out;
CartoonDeformNoNormals
struct VS_OUTPUT_QUANT
float4 Pos           : POSITION0;
float4 vDiffuse
 : COLOR;
float2 TexCoord      : TEXCOORD0;
float2 TexCoord1     : TEXCOORD1;
 float4x4  ViewProjX;
   // obj->clip
 float4    light0Pos;
    
 float4    light1Pos;
    
 float4    lightDir;
    
 float4    materialColor;
 float     light0Intensity;
 float     light1Intensity;
 float     ambientLightIntensity;
 float
lightDirIntensity;
// bone palette
 float4x4  bonesPalette[18];
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT VS_main( float4 inPos: POSITION0, float3 inNormal: NORMAL0,float2 inTexCoord : TEXCOORD0, 
  float3 blendWeight: BLENDWEIGHT0, float4 blendIndices : COLOR)
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT Out;
float4 scaler
= {64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f };
float4 scaledIndices
blendIndices * scaler;
float4 skinPos 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
float4 skinPos1 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
float4 skinPos2 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalPos = skinPos + skinPos1 + skinPos2;
//float4 skinFinalPos.w = 1.0f;
float4 skinNorm 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
float4 skinNorm1 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
float4 skinNorm2 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalNorm = skinNorm + skinNorm1 + skinNorm2;
Out.Pos       =  mul( skinFinalPos,  ViewProjX  );
float3 lightVector0 = (light0Pos - skinFinalPos);
float3 lightVectorN0 = normalize(lightVector0);
float3 lightVector1 = (light1Pos - skinFinalPos);
float3 lightVectorN1 = normalize(lightVector1);
// compute lighting
float  diffuse
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm,lightVectorN0)) * light0Intensity);
float  diffuse1
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm,lightVectorN1)) * light1Intensity);
float  directional
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm,lightDir.xyz))  * lightDirIntensity);
Out.TexCoord.x
= min(1.0f, (diffuse + diffuse1 + directional + ambientLightIntensity));
Out.TexCoord.y
= 0.0f;
Out.vDiffuse
= materialColor;
Out.TexCoord1
= inTexCoord;
return Out;

struct VS_OUTPUT_QUANT
float4 Pos           : POSITION0;
float4 vDiffuse
 : COLOR;
float2 TexCoord      : TEXCOORD0;
float2 TexCoord1     : TEXCOORD1;
 float4x4  ViewProjX;
   // obj->clip
 float4    light0Pos;
    
 float4    light1Pos;
    
 float4    lightDir;
    
 float4    materialColor;
 float     light0Intensity;
 float     light1Intensity;
 float     ambientLightIntensity;
 float
lightDirIntensity;
 float4x4
WorldXf;
   // obj->world
 float4x4
modelViewXf;   // obj->view
 float
silhouetteSize; 
 float4x4
ViewWorldXf;   // obj->viewWorld
// bone palette
 float4x4  bonesPalette[18];
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT VS_main( float4 inPos: POSITION0, float3 inNormal: NORMAL0,float2 inTexCoord : TEXCOORD0, 
  float3 blendWeight: BLENDWEIGHT0, float4 blendIndices : COLOR, float3 inNomral2 : NORMAL1)
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT Out;
float4 scaler
= {64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f, 64.0f };
float4 inPosScale
= ( 1.0f - silhouetteSize );
float4 scaledIndices
blendIndices * scaler;
float4 skinPos 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
float4 skinPos1 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
float4 skinPos2 
= mul( inPos, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalPos = skinPos + skinPos1 + skinPos2;
//float4 skinFinalPos.w = 1.0f;
float4 skinNorm 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
float4 skinNorm1 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
float4 skinNorm2 
= mul( inNormal, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalNorm
= skinNorm + skinNorm1 + skinNorm2;
skinNorm 
= mul( inNomral2, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.z])
* blendWeight.xxxx;
skinNorm1 
= mul( inNomral2, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.y])
* blendWeight.yyyy;
skinNorm2 
= mul( inNomral2, bonesPalette[scaledIndices.x])
* blendWeight.zzzz;
float4 skinFinalNorm2
= skinNorm + skinNorm1 + skinNorm2;
float4 worldPos
= mul( skinFinalPos,  WorldXf  );
float4 worldViewNormal
= mul( skinFinalNorm,  modelViewXf  );
float4 scaledNormal
= -worldViewNormal * inPosScale;
   float4 worldNormalOffset
= mul( scaledNormal,  ViewWorldXf  );
float4 finalWorldPos
= worldPos + worldNormalOffset;
// to view projection
Out.Pos
= mul(finalWorldPos, ViewProjX);
float3 lightVector0 = (light0Pos - finalWorldPos);
float3 lightVectorN0 = normalize(lightVector0);
float3 lightVector1 = (light1Pos - finalWorldPos);
float3 lightVectorN1 = normalize(lightVector1);
// compute lighting
float  diffuse
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm2,lightVectorN0)) * light0Intensity);
float  diffuse1
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm2,lightVectorN1)) * light1Intensity);
float  directional
= (max(0,dot(skinFinalNorm2,lightDir.xyz))  * lightDirIntensity);
Out.TexCoord.x
= min(1.0f, (diffuse + diffuse1 + directional + ambientLightIntensity));
Out.TexCoord.y
= 0.0f;
Out.vDiffuse
= materialColor;
Out.TexCoord1
= inTexCoord;
return Out;

struct VS_OUTPUT_QUANT
float4 Pos           : POSITION0;
float4 vDiffuse
 : COLOR;

 float4    light1Pos;

 float     light1Intensity;
 float     ambientLightIntensity;
 float
lightDirIntensity;
 float
silhouetteSize; 
 float4x4
WorldXf;
   // obj->world
 float4x4  ViewProjX;
   // obj->clip
 float4x4
modelViewXf;   // obj->view
 float4x4
ViewWorldXf;   // obj->viewWorld
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT VS_main( float4 inPos: POSITION0, float3 inNormal: NORMAL0,float2 inTexCoord : TEXCOORD0, float3 inNomral2 : NORMAL1 ) 
VS_OUTPUT_QUANT Out;
float4 inPosScale
= ( 1.0f - silhouetteSize );
float4 worldPos
= mul( inPos,  WorldXf  );
   // transform normal
float4 worldViewNormal
= mul( inNormal,  modelViewXf  );
float4 scaledNormal
= -worldViewNormal * inPosScale;
float4 worldNormalOffset
= mul( scaledNormal,  ViewWorldXf  );
float4 finalWorldPos
= worldPos    + worldNormalOffset;
Out.Pos
=  mul( finalWorldPos,  ViewProjX  );
float3 lightVector0
= (light0Pos - worldPos);
float3 lightVectorN0
= normalize(lightVector0);
float3 lightVector1
= (light1Pos - worldPos);
float3 lightVectorN1
= normalize(lightVector1);
float3 normU
= normalize(inNomral2);
// compute lighting
float  diffuse
= (max(0,dot(normU,lightVectorN0)) * light0Intensity);
float  diffuse1
= (max(0,dot(normU,lightVectorN1)) * light1Intensity);
float  directional
= (max(0,dot(normU,lightDir.xyz))  * lightDirIntensity);
Out.TexCoord.x
=  min(1.0f, (diffuse + diffuse1 + directional + ambientLightIntensity));
Out.TexCoord.y
= 0.0f;
Out.vDiffuse
= materialColor;
Out.TexCoord1
= inTexCoord;
return Out;
